  <COMMENT line1="154" col1="1" line2="154" col2="68" start="16941" end="17008">#' A simple helper function that makes a so-called "MA-plot", i.e. a</COMMENT>

  <COMMENT line1="158" col1="1" line2="158" col2="61" start="17381" end="17441">#' This function is essentially two lines of code: building a</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="159" col1="1" line2="159" col2="65" start="17491" end="17555">#' \code{data.frame} and passing this to the \code{plotMA} method</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="160" col1="1" line2="160" col2="54" start="17601" end="17654">#' for \code{data.frame} from the geneplotter package.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="161" col1="1" line2="161" col2="74" start="17711" end="17784">#' The code was modified in version 1.28 to change from red to blue points</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="162" col1="1" line2="162" col2="75" start="17821" end="17895">#' for better visibility for users with color-blindness. The original plots</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="163" col1="1" line2="163" col2="74" start="17931" end="18004">#' can still be made via the use of \code{returnData=TRUE} and passing the</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="164" col1="1" line2="164" col2="63" start="18041" end="18103">#' resulting data.frame directly to \code{geneplotter::plotMA}.</COMMENT>
